 1
 Baking sodasodium carbonate is known in simple terms as baking soda

 Alum is a phytocarp astringent and also has anti-septic properties
 yah bacteria ko badhane se rokatii he

 ye sab kuch ek saath ho rahaa he

 Something similar changes us Sudhir Saxena's poetic collection 'ishwar yes, no
 
 
 to' main dikhataa he
 Sudhir takes the very latest and updated subject of the poem, forcing the readers to shudder and contemplate deep meditation
 kavy sangrah ke sheershak se hi kavitaaon ke swaroop kaa, bhav kaa, dher saare tark vitark or prashnon kaa saakshaatkaar ho jaataa he
 The title itself is a mixed barrage of doubts and arguments
 donon hi baaten ek saath kahi gai hai
 In the same sentence, two expressions are used in sarcasm
 'haa or nahin' ye virodhabhas jivan ke har kshetra main hamaare saamne jhulata he
 It is obvious that where there is talk of power like God, it is only natural to come to this state of mind
 asti or naasti par yugon se manthan hote aayaa he or ho rahaa he par abhi tak na to asti kaa pramaan mila he na hi naasti kaa
 Therefore the poet is also swinging between yes and no
 aastikon ke apane tark hai ishwar ko maanane ke or naastikon ke apane tark hai ishwar ko na maanane ke
 Let us see what Sudhir Saxena's arguments are? What is the evidence? With the title, the mystic tendency of the poet emerges
 kavi ek taraf ishwar ke astitv ko sweekaarta dikhaai detaa he
 On the other hand, there has been denial but this denial is also not complete denial
 nahin kehane ke baad bhi kavi ke man main kuch chalata he
 The title itself has so much mystery, questions, arguments, arguments, brainstorming that the reader is stuck here and he himself becomes a victim of this brainstorm
 is kavy sangrah main 36 kavitaayen hai
 In 'god only if God knows the language / and it is so far from us', the poet has told God far away from us
 jaise dur khadey vyakti ko hamaari aawaaj sunai nahi detii, thik vaise hi ishwar bhi hamase itani dur he ki us tak hamaari aawaaj nahin pahunch paati
 So it is not possible to talk to him
 is samvadaheenata kaa ek or tark kavi ne diya he ki ishwar hamaari bhashaa bhi nahin jaanata, na ham uski bhashaa jaanate hai to yaa to vah bahubhashi ho jaae yaa ham hi ho jate hai
 Since God does not know our language, if we send a document of our sorrows to him, he will not be able to read
 na hi kisi vidhi se hamaari aawaaj pahunchane par koi pratikriya vyakt kar sakegaa kyonki wo hamaari bhashaa hi nahin jaanata
 In the second verse, the poet satirizes the god by explaining the raga-color-interests of God that he means 'just' with classical music
 use puraatan chijen pasand he jo ki is yug main zyada vyavhaar main nahin rah gai, jaise sashtaang pranaam karnaa, aadi
 Further in this poem, the poet says that with time the environment has also changed, as was the time of God
 aise main ishwar ke liye apane astitv ko bachaae rakhana bahut mushkil he
 In the third verse, the poet has targeted the birth of God or, say, the origin of the earth, that even after billions of years, if he had compassion in God, he must have been sad
 prithvi par jo vinaash or narsanhaar hua he yaa jo krurta kii paribhaasha di gai he, chaahe vah baahar ke akramanakariyon kii ore se ho yaa desh ke andar hi hui mahabharat ho, ishwar un par jarur dukhi hua hoga

 Political history of Khajuraho seat: Ram Sahay of Congress won the first election held in 1957 in Khajuraho Lok Sabha seat
 1957 main yahaan par phir se chunaav hue jisamen congress ke hi motilal malviya vijayi rahi
 In its next election in 1962, the Congress scored a hat-trick of victories here and Ram Sahai once again became an MP
